Book Details Page - **Route Path**: `/book/<int:book_id>` - **Function Name**: `book_details` - **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST - **Template Rendered**: `book_details.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `book` (dict): Fields - `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `price`(float), `description`(str), `stock`(int)   - `reviews` (list of dict): Each dict: `review_id`(int), `customer_name`(str), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str), `review_date`(str)  - **POST Handling**:   - When form or AJAX call to add book to cart (triggered by `add-to-cart-button`), add the book with quantity=1 to `cart.txt` or update quantity if exists.   - Redirect or reload page after POST.  ---  ### 5. Shopping Cart Page - **Route Path**: `/cart` - **Function Name**: `cart` - **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST - **Template Rendered**: `cart.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `cart_items` (list of dict): Each dict: `cart_id`(int), `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `quantity`(int), `price`(float), `subtotal`(float)   - `total_amount` (float): Sum of all subtotals  - **POST Handling**:   - Form submissions can update quantities (`update-quantity-{item_id}` inputs) or remove items (`remove-item-button-{item_id}` buttons).   - Update or remove cart items in `cart.txt` accordingly.   - Redirect after POST.  ---  ### 6. Checkout Page - **Route Path**: `/checkout` - **Function Name**: `checkout` - **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST - **Template Rendered**: `checkout.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `cart_items` (list of dict): Same as cart page   - `total_amount` (float): Sum of cart item subtotals  - **POST Handling**:   - Process order submission with form fields:     - `customer_name` (str), `shipping_address` (str), `payment_method` (str from "Credit Card", "PayPal", "Bank Transfer")   - Create new order in `orders.txt`, and create corresponding entries in `order_items.txt`.   - Clear cart items from `cart.txt`.   - Redirect to `/order_history`  ---  ### 7. Order History Page - **Route Path**: `/order_history` - **Function Name**: `order_history` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: `order_history.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `orders` (list of dict): Each dict: `order_id`(int), `customer_name`(str), `order_date`(str), `total_amount`(float), `status`(str), `shipping_address`(str)   - `status_filter` (str): One of "All", "Pending", "Shipped", "Delivered" (default "All")  - **Filtering**: Apply filter by `status` query parameter  ---  ### 8. Order Details Page (Optional but beneficial for `/order_history` view button) - **Route Path**: `/order/<int:order_id>` - **Function Name**: `order_details` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: `order_details.html` (not explicitly requested in user task but inferred to view order details) - **Context Variables**:   - `order` (dict): Same fields as `orders` above   - `order_items` (list of dict): Each dict: `order_item_id`(int), `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `quantity`(int), `price`(float), `subtotal`(float)  ---  ### 9. Reviews Page - **Route Path**: `/reviews` - **Function Name**: `reviews` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: `reviews.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `reviews` (list of dict): Each dict: `review_id`(int), `book_title`(str), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str)   - `rating_filter` (str): Rating filter from query param, e.g. "All", "5", "4", ...  - **Filtering**: Use `rating` query param to filter reviews  ---  ### 10. Write Review Page - **Route Path**: `/write_review` - **Function Name**: `write_review` - **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST - **Template Rendered**: `write_review.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `purchasable_books` (list of dict): Purchased books available for review with fields: `book_id`(int), `title`(str)  - **POST Handling**:   - Form fields: `book_id` (int), `rating` (int 1-5), `review_text` (str), `customer_name` (Str, can be static or asked elsewise, no auth is specified, assumed user name submission with review or fixed name)   - Append to `reviews.txt` with new review_id   - Redirect to `/reviews`  ---  ### 11. Bestsellers Page - **Route Path**: `/bestsellers` - **Function Name**: `bestsellers` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: `bestsellers.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `bestsellers` (list of dict): Each dict: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `sales_count`(int)   - `time_period` (str): Filter by period from query param ("This Week", "This Month", "All Time")  - **Filtering**: Use query param for time period filter   ---  ## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification  ### 1. Dashboard Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/dashboard.html` - **Page Title**: `Bookstore Dashboard` - **Main H1**: `Bookstore Dashboard` - **Element IDs**:   - `dashboard-page` (Div): Container div for dashboard   - `featured-books` (Div): Displays featured book recommendations   - `browse-catalog-button` (Button): Navigates to `/catalog`   - `view-cart-button` (Button): Navigates to `/cart`   - `bestsellers-button` (Button): Navigates to `/bestsellers` - **Context Variables**:   - `featured_books` (list of dict)   - `bestsellers` (list of dict) - **Navigation**:   - `browse-catalog-button` calls `url_for('catalog')`   - `view-cart-button` calls `url_for('cart')`   - `bestsellers-button` calls `url_for('bestsellers')` - **Implementation notes**:   - List featured books with title, author, and price inside `featured-books` div.   - Display bestsellers (top ranked) with rank, title, author, sales count.  ---  ### 2. Book Catalog Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/catalog.html` - **Page Title**: `Book Catalog` - **Main H1**: `Book Catalog` - **Element IDs**:   - `catalog-page` (Div): Container div   - `search-input` (Input): Text input for search query   - `category-filter` (Dropdown select): For category filtering   - `books-grid` (Div): Holds book cards   - Dynamic: `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): In each book card, to view details - **Context Variables**:   - `books` (list of dict)   - `categories` (list of dict)   - `selected_category` (str or None)   - `search_query` (str or None) - **Navigation**:   - Book detail buttons use `url_for('book_details', book_id=book['book_id'])` - **Filtering/Search**:   - Search input and category dropdown submit on change or submit button to reload page with query params.  ---  ### 3. Book Details Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/book_details.html` - **Page Title**: `Book Details` - **Main H1**: `book['title']` (dynamic) - **Element IDs**:   - `book-details-page` (Div): Container   - `book-title` (H1): Displays book title dynamically   - `book-author` (Div): Displays author   - `book-price` (Div): Displays price   - `add-to-cart-button` (Button): Adds book to cart via POST   - `book-reviews` (Div): Lists customer reviews - **Context Variables**:   - `book` (dict)   - `reviews` (list of dict) - **POST Form**:    - Wrap the add to cart button inside a form with method POST.   - Include hidden input for `book_id`.  ---  ### 4. Shopping Cart Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/cart.html` - **Page Title**: `Shopping Cart` - **Main H1**: `Shopping Cart` - **Element IDs**:   - `cart-page` (Div): Container   - `cart-items-table` (Table): Lists cart items with columns: Title, Quantity, Price, Subtotal   - Dynamic inputs: `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input number) for quantity   - Dynamic buttons: `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button) to remove item   - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button): Navigates to `/checkout`   - `total-amount` (Div): Displays total cart amount - **Context Variables**:   - `cart_items` (list of dict)   - `total_amount` (float) - **POST Form**:   - Wrap the cart items table in a form with method POST.   - Each quantity input named as `quantity_{cart_id}` to update quantities.   - Each remove button named as `remove_{cart_id}`.  ---  ### 5. Checkout Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/checkout.html` - **Page Title**: `Checkout` - **Main H1**: `Checkout` - **Element IDs**:   - `checkout-page` (Div): Container   - `customer-name` (Input): For customer name   - `shipping-address` (Textarea): For address   - `payment-method` (Dropdown select): Options - Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer   - `place-order-button` (Button): To submit form - **Context Variables**:   - `cart_items` (list of dict)   - `total_amount` (float) - **POST Form**:   - All inputs and button inside a form method POST.  ---  ### 6. Order History Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/order_history.html` - **Page Title**: `Order History` - **Main H1**: `Order History` - **Element IDs**:   - `orders-page` (Div): Container   - `orders-table` (Table): Columns - Order ID, Date, Total Amount, Status   - Dynamic buttons: `view-order-button-{order_id}`   - `order-status-filter` (Dropdown): Filters by order status   - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates to `/dashboard` - **Context Variables**:   - `orders` (list of dict)   - `status_filter` (str) - **Navigation**:   - View order buttons link to `/order/<order_id>` (if implemented) or can be a placeholder.  ---  ### 7. Reviews Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/reviews.html` - **Page Title**: `Customer Reviews` - **Main H1**: `Customer Reviews` - **Element IDs**:   - `reviews-page` (Div): Container   - `reviews-list` (Div): Lists reviews with book title, rating, review text   - `write-review-button` (Button): Navigates to `/write_review`   - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown): Filters reviews by rating   - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates to `/dashboard` - **Context Variables**:   - `reviews` (list of dict)   - `rating_filter` (str) - **Navigation**:   - `write-review-button` calls `url_for('write_review')`  ---  ### 8. Write Review Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/write_review.html` - **Page Title**: `Write a Review` - **Main H1**: `Write a Review` - **Element IDs**:   - `write-review-page` (Div): Container   - `select-book` (Dropdown select): To select book to review   - `rating-select` (Dropdown select): Ratings from 1 to 5   - `review-text` (Textarea): For review text   - `submit-review-button` (Button): Submit review - **Context Variables**:   - `purchasable_books` (list of dict) - **POST Form**:   - All inputs and submit button inside a form method POST.  ---  ### 9. Bestsellers Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/bestsellers.html` - **Page Title**: `Bestsellers` - **Main H1**: `Bestsellers` - **Element IDs**:   - `bestsellers-page` (Div): Container   - `bestsellers-list` (Div): Ranked list of bestsellers with rank, title, author, sales count   - `time-period-filter` (Dropdown): Select period - This Week, This Month, All Time   - Dynamic: `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): View book details   - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates to `/dashboard` - **Context Variables**:   - `bestsellers` (list of dict)   - `time_period` (str) - **Navigation**:   - Buttons link to `url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)`  ---  ## Section 3: Data Schemas Specification  ### 1. Books Data - **File Location**: `data/books.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `book_id` (int): Unique ID   - `title` (str): Book title   - `author` (str): Author name   - `isbn` (str): ISBN number   - `category` (str): Book category   - `price` (float): Price in dollars   - `stock` (int): Number of copies in stock   - `description` (str): Short book description - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel   2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind   3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction   ```  ---  ### 2. Categories Data - **File Location**: `data/categories.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   category_id|category_name|description   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `category_id` (int): Unique ID   - `category_name` (str): Category name   - `description` (str): Description of category - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels   2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books   3|Science|Scientific topics and research   ```  ---  ### 3. Cart Data - **File Location**: `data/cart.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   cart_id|book_id|quantity|added_date   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `cart_id` (int): Unique cart item ID   - `book_id` (int): Book reference   - `quantity` (int): Quantity selected   - `added_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD): Date added to cart - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|1|2|2025-01-15   2|3|1|2025-01-16   ```  ---  ### 4. Orders Data - **File Location**: `data/orders.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   order_id|customer_name|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `order_id` (int): Unique order ID   - `customer_name` (str): Name of customer   - `order_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD): Date of order   - `total_amount` (float): Total order amount   - `status` (str): Order status (Pending, Shipped, Delivered)   - `shipping_address` (str): Shipping address - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001   2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001   ```  ---  ### 5. Order Items Data - **File Location**: `data/order_items.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `order_item_id` (int): Unique ID for order item   - `order_id` (int): Related order ID   - `book_id` (int): Book reference   - `quantity` (int): Quantity ordered   - `price` (float): Price at time of purchase - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|1|1|2|12.99   2|1|3|1|14.99   3|2|2|1|16.99   ```  ---  ### 6. Reviews Data - **File Location**: `data/reviews.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `review_id` (int): Unique review ID   - `book_id` (int): Book reviewed   - `customer_name` (str): Name of reviewer   - `rating` (int): Rating 1 to 5   - `review_text` (str): Text of review   - `review_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD): Date of review - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12   2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13   3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15   ```  ---  ### 7. Bestsellers Data - **File Location**: `data/bestsellers.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   book_id|sales_count|period   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `book_id` (int): Book reference   - `sales_count` (int): Number of sales   - `period` (str): Time period (e.g., "This Week", "This Month", "All Time") - **Example Rows**:   ```   2|150|This Month   1|120|This Month   3|95|This Month   ```  ---  # End of Design Specification

[DEBUG] Review Content for FrontendDeveloper_Failover_Reliable -> SystemArchitect:
  [design_spec.md] # BookstoreOnline Design Specification  ---  ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification  ### 1. Root Route - **Route Path**: `/` - **Function Name**: `root_redirect` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: None (Redirect) - **Context Variables**: None - **Behavior**: Redirects permanently (HTTP 302) to `/dashboard`  ---  ### 2. Dashboard Page - **Route Path**: `/dashboard` - **Function Name**: `dashboard` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: `dashboard.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `featured_books` (list of dict): Each dict contains book fields: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `price`(float), `cover_url`(str, optional if used)   - `bestsellers` (list of dict): Each dict: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `sales_count`(int)  ---  ### 3. Book Catalog Page - **Route Path**: `/catalog` - **Function Name**: `catalog` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: `catalog.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `books` (list of dict): Each dict: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `price`(float)   - `categories` (list of dict): Each dict: `category_id`(int), `category_name`(str)   - `selected_category` (str or None): Name of category filtered or None   - `search_query` (str or None): Search string or None  - **Search and Filtering**: Use query parameters `search` and `category` to filter books by title, author, or ISBN and category  ---  ### 4. Book Details Page - **Route Path**: `/book/<int:book_id>` - **Function Name**: `book_details` - **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST - **Template Rendered**: `book_details.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `book` (dict): Fields - `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `price`(float), `description`(str), `stock`(int)   - `reviews` (list of dict): Each dict: `review_id`(int), `customer_name`(str), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str), `review_date`(str)  - **POST Handling**:   - When form or AJAX call to add book to cart (triggered by `add-to-cart-button`), add the book with quantity=1 to `cart.txt` or update quantity if exists.   - Redirect or reload page after POST.  ---  ### 5. Shopping Cart Page - **Route Path**: `/cart` - **Function Name**: `cart` - **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST - **Template Rendered**: `cart.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `cart_items` (list of dict): Each dict: `cart_id`(int), `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `quantity`(int), `price`(float), `subtotal`(float)   - `total_amount` (float): Sum of all subtotals  - **POST Handling**:   - Form submissions can update quantities (`update-quantity-{item_id}` inputs) or remove items (`remove-item-button-{item_id}` buttons).   - Update or remove cart items in `cart.txt` accordingly.   - Redirect after POST.  ---  ### 6. Checkout Page - **Route Path**: `/checkout` - **Function Name**: `checkout` - **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST - **Template Rendered**: `checkout.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `cart_items` (list of dict): Same as cart page   - `total_amount` (float): Sum of cart item subtotals  - **POST Handling**:   - Process order submission with form fields:     - `customer_name` (str), `shipping_address` (str), `payment_method` (str from "Credit Card", "PayPal", "Bank Transfer")   - Create new order in `orders.txt`, and create corresponding entries in `order_items.txt`.   - Clear cart items from `cart.txt`.   - Redirect to `/order_history`  ---  ### 7. Order History Page - **Route Path**: `/order_history` - **Function Name**: `order_history` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: `order_history.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `orders` (list of dict): Each dict: `order_id`(int), `customer_name`(str), `order_date`(str), `total_amount`(float), `status`(str), `shipping_address`(str)   - `status_filter` (str): One of "All", "Pending", "Shipped", "Delivered" (default "All")  - **Filtering**: Apply filter by `status` query parameter  ---  ### 8. Order Details Page (Optional but beneficial for `/order_history` view button) - **Route Path**: `/order/<int:order_id>` - **Function Name**: `order_details` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: `order_details.html` (not explicitly requested in user task but inferred to view order details) - **Context Variables**:   - `order` (dict): Same fields as `orders` above   - `order_items` (list of dict): Each dict: `order_item_id`(int), `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `quantity`(int), `price`(float), `subtotal`(float)  ---  ### 9. Reviews Page - **Route Path**: `/reviews` - **Function Name**: `reviews` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: `reviews.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `reviews` (list of dict): Each dict: `review_id`(int), `book_title`(str), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str)   - `rating_filter` (str): Rating filter from query param, e.g. "All", "5", "4", ...  - **Filtering**: Use `rating` query param to filter reviews  ---  ### 10. Write Review Page - **Route Path**: `/write_review` - **Function Name**: `write_review` - **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST - **Template Rendered**: `write_review.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `purchasable_books` (list of dict): Purchased books available for review with fields: `book_id`(int), `title`(str)  - **POST Handling**:   - Form fields: `book_id` (int), `rating` (int 1-5), `review_text` (str), `customer_name` (Str, can be static or asked elsewise, no auth is specified, assumed user name submission with review or fixed name)   - Append to `reviews.txt` with new review_id   - Redirect to `/reviews`  ---  ### 11. Bestsellers Page - **Route Path**: `/bestsellers` - **Function Name**: `bestsellers` - **HTTP Methods**: GET - **Template Rendered**: `bestsellers.html` - **Context Variables**:   - `bestsellers` (list of dict): Each dict: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `sales_count`(int)   - `time_period` (str): Filter by period from query param ("This Week", "This Month", "All Time")  - **Filtering**: Use query param for time period filter   ---  ## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification  ### 1. Dashboard Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/dashboard.html` - **Page Title**: `Bookstore Dashboard` - **Main H1**: `Bookstore Dashboard` - **Element IDs**:   - `dashboard-page` (Div): Container div for dashboard   - `featured-books` (Div): Displays featured book recommendations   - `browse-catalog-button` (Button): Navigates to `/catalog`   - `view-cart-button` (Button): Navigates to `/cart`   - `bestsellers-button` (Button): Navigates to `/bestsellers` - **Context Variables**:   - `featured_books` (list of dict)   - `bestsellers` (list of dict) - **Navigation**:   - `browse-catalog-button` calls `url_for('catalog')`   - `view-cart-button` calls `url_for('cart')`   - `bestsellers-button` calls `url_for('bestsellers')` - **Implementation notes**:   - List featured books with title, author, and price inside `featured-books` div.   - Display bestsellers (top ranked) with rank, title, author, sales count.  ---  ### 2. Book Catalog Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/catalog.html` - **Page Title**: `Book Catalog` - **Main H1**: `Book Catalog` - **Element IDs**:   - `catalog-page` (Div): Container div   - `search-input` (Input): Text input for search query   - `category-filter` (Dropdown select): For category filtering   - `books-grid` (Div): Holds book cards   - Dynamic: `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): In each book card, to view details - **Context Variables**:   - `books` (list of dict)   - `categories` (list of dict)   - `selected_category` (str or None)   - `search_query` (str or None) - **Navigation**:   - Book detail buttons use `url_for('book_details', book_id=book['book_id'])` - **Filtering/Search**:   - Search input and category dropdown submit on change or submit button to reload page with query params.  ---  ### 3. Book Details Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/book_details.html` - **Page Title**: `Book Details` - **Main H1**: `book['title']` (dynamic) - **Element IDs**:   - `book-details-page` (Div): Container   - `book-title` (H1): Displays book title dynamically   - `book-author` (Div): Displays author   - `book-price` (Div): Displays price   - `add-to-cart-button` (Button): Adds book to cart via POST   - `book-reviews` (Div): Lists customer reviews - **Context Variables**:   - `book` (dict)   - `reviews` (list of dict) - **POST Form**:    - Wrap the add to cart button inside a form with method POST.   - Include hidden input for `book_id`.  ---  ### 4. Shopping Cart Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/cart.html` - **Page Title**: `Shopping Cart` - **Main H1**: `Shopping Cart` - **Element IDs**:   - `cart-page` (Div): Container   - `cart-items-table` (Table): Lists cart items with columns: Title, Quantity, Price, Subtotal   - Dynamic inputs: `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input number) for quantity   - Dynamic buttons: `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button) to remove item   - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button): Navigates to `/checkout`   - `total-amount` (Div): Displays total cart amount - **Context Variables**:   - `cart_items` (list of dict)   - `total_amount` (float) - **POST Form**:   - Wrap the cart items table in a form with method POST.   - Each quantity input named as `quantity_{cart_id}` to update quantities.   - Each remove button named as `remove_{cart_id}`.  ---  ### 5. Checkout Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/checkout.html` - **Page Title**: `Checkout` - **Main H1**: `Checkout` - **Element IDs**:   - `checkout-page` (Div): Container   - `customer-name` (Input): For customer name   - `shipping-address` (Textarea): For address   - `payment-method` (Dropdown select): Options - Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer   - `place-order-button` (Button): To submit form - **Context Variables**:   - `cart_items` (list of dict)   - `total_amount` (float) - **POST Form**:   - All inputs and button inside a form method POST.  ---  ### 6. Order History Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/order_history.html` - **Page Title**: `Order History` - **Main H1**: `Order History` - **Element IDs**:   - `orders-page` (Div): Container   - `orders-table` (Table): Columns - Order ID, Date, Total Amount, Status   - Dynamic buttons: `view-order-button-{order_id}`   - `order-status-filter` (Dropdown): Filters by order status   - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates to `/dashboard` - **Context Variables**:   - `orders` (list of dict)   - `status_filter` (str) - **Navigation**:   - View order buttons link to `/order/<order_id>` (if implemented) or can be a placeholder.  ---  ### 7. Reviews Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/reviews.html` - **Page Title**: `Customer Reviews` - **Main H1**: `Customer Reviews` - **Element IDs**:   - `reviews-page` (Div): Container   - `reviews-list` (Div): Lists reviews with book title, rating, review text   - `write-review-button` (Button): Navigates to `/write_review`   - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown): Filters reviews by rating   - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates to `/dashboard` - **Context Variables**:   - `reviews` (list of dict)   - `rating_filter` (str) - **Navigation**:   - `write-review-button` calls `url_for('write_review')`  ---  ### 8. Write Review Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/write_review.html` - **Page Title**: `Write a Review` - **Main H1**: `Write a Review` - **Element IDs**:   - `write-review-page` (Div): Container   - `select-book` (Dropdown select): To select book to review   - `rating-select` (Dropdown select): Ratings from 1 to 5   - `review-text` (Textarea): For review text   - `submit-review-button` (Button): Submit review - **Context Variables**:   - `purchasable_books` (list of dict) - **POST Form**:   - All inputs and submit button inside a form method POST.  ---  ### 9. Bestsellers Page Template - **File Path**: `templates/bestsellers.html` - **Page Title**: `Bestsellers` - **Main H1**: `Bestsellers` - **Element IDs**:   - `bestsellers-page` (Div): Container   - `bestsellers-list` (Div): Ranked list of bestsellers with rank, title, author, sales count   - `time-period-filter` (Dropdown): Select period - This Week, This Month, All Time   - Dynamic: `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): View book details   - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates to `/dashboard` - **Context Variables**:   - `bestsellers` (list of dict)   - `time_period` (str) - **Navigation**:   - Buttons link to `url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)`  ---  ## Section 3: Data Schemas Specification  ### 1. Books Data - **File Location**: `data/books.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `book_id` (int): Unique ID   - `title` (str): Book title   - `author` (str): Author name   - `isbn` (str): ISBN number   - `category` (str): Book category   - `price` (float): Price in dollars   - `stock` (int): Number of copies in stock   - `description` (str): Short book description - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel   2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind   3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction   ```  ---  ### 2. Categories Data - **File Location**: `data/categories.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   category_id|category_name|description   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `category_id` (int): Unique ID   - `category_name` (str): Category name   - `description` (str): Description of category - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels   2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books   3|Science|Scientific topics and research   ```  ---  ### 3. Cart Data - **File Location**: `data/cart.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   cart_id|book_id|quantity|added_date   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `cart_id` (int): Unique cart item ID   - `book_id` (int): Book reference   - `quantity` (int): Quantity selected   - `added_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD): Date added to cart - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|1|2|2025-01-15   2|3|1|2025-01-16   ```  ---  ### 4. Orders Data - **File Location**: `data/orders.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   order_id|customer_name|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `order_id` (int): Unique order ID   - `customer_name` (str): Name of customer   - `order_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD): Date of order   - `total_amount` (float): Total order amount   - `status` (str): Order status (Pending, Shipped, Delivered)   - `shipping_address` (str): Shipping address - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001   2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001   ```  ---  ### 5. Order Items Data - **File Location**: `data/order_items.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `order_item_id` (int): Unique ID for order item   - `order_id` (int): Related order ID   - `book_id` (int): Book reference   - `quantity` (int): Quantity ordered   - `price` (float): Price at time of purchase - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|1|1|2|12.99   2|1|3|1|14.99   3|2|2|1|16.99   ```  ---  ### 6. Reviews Data - **File Location**: `data/reviews.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `review_id` (int): Unique review ID   - `book_id` (int): Book reviewed   - `customer_name` (str): Name of reviewer   - `rating` (int): Rating 1 to 5   - `review_text` (str): Text of review   - `review_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD): Date of review - **Example Rows**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12   2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13   3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15   ```  ---  ### 7. Bestsellers Data - **File Location**: `data/bestsellers.txt` - **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:   ```   book_id|sales_count|period   ``` - **Field Descriptions**:   - `book_id` (int): Book reference   - `sales_count` (int): Number of sales   - `period` (str): Time period (e.g., "This Week", "This Month", "All Time") - **Example Rows**:   ```   2|150|This Month   1|120|This Month   3|95|This Month   ```  ---  # End of Design Specification

# BookstoreOnline Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

### 1. Root Route
- **Route Path**: `/`
- **Function Name**: `root_redirect`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET
- **Template Rendered**: None (Redirect)
- **Context Variables**: None
- **Behavior**: Redirects permanently (HTTP 302) to `/dashboard`

---

### 2. Dashboard Page
- **Route Path**: `/dashboard`
- **Function Name**: `dashboard`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET
- **Template Rendered**: `dashboard.html`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `featured_books` (list of dict): Each dict contains book fields: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `price`(float), `cover_url`(str, optional if used)
  - `bestsellers` (list of dict): Each dict: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `sales_count`(int)

---

### 3. Book Catalog Page
- **Route Path**: `/catalog`
- **Function Name**: `catalog`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET
- **Template Rendered**: `catalog.html`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `books` (list of dict): Each dict: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `price`(float)
  - `categories` (list of dict): Each dict: `category_id`(int), `category_name`(str)
  - `selected_category` (str or None): Name of category filtered or None
  - `search_query` (str or None): Search string or None

- **Search and Filtering**: Use query parameters `search` and `category` to filter books by title, author, or ISBN and category

---

### 4. Book Details Page
- **Route Path**: `/book/<int:book_id>`
- **Function Name**: `book_details`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST
- **Template Rendered**: `book_details.html`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `book` (dict): Fields - `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `price`(float), `description`(str), `stock`(int)
  - `reviews` (list of dict): Each dict: `review_id`(int), `customer_name`(str), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str), `review_date`(str)

- **POST Handling**:
  - When form or AJAX call to add book to cart (triggered by `add-to-cart-button`), add the book with quantity=1 to `cart.txt` or update quantity if exists.
  - Redirect or reload page after POST.

---

### 5. Shopping Cart Page
- **Route Path**: `/cart`
- **Function Name**: `cart`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST
- **Template Rendered**: `cart.html`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `cart_items` (list of dict): Each dict: `cart_id`(int), `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `quantity`(int), `price`(float), `subtotal`(float)
  - `total_amount` (float): Sum of all subtotals

- **POST Handling**:
  - Form submissions can update quantities (`update-quantity-{item_id}` inputs) or remove items (`remove-item-button-{item_id}` buttons).
  - Update or remove cart items in `cart.txt` accordingly.
  - Redirect after POST.

---

### 6. Checkout Page
- **Route Path**: `/checkout`
- **Function Name**: `checkout`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST
- **Template Rendered**: `checkout.html`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `cart_items` (list of dict): Same as cart page
  - `total_amount` (float): Sum of cart item subtotals

- **POST Handling**:
  - Process order submission with form fields:
    - `customer_name` (str), `shipping_address` (str), `payment_method` (str from "Credit Card", "PayPal", "Bank Transfer")
  - Create new order in `orders.txt`, and create corresponding entries in `order_items.txt`.
  - Clear cart items from `cart.txt`.
  - Redirect to `/order_history`

---

### 7. Order History Page
- **Route Path**: `/order_history`
- **Function Name**: `order_history`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET
- **Template Rendered**: `order_history.html`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `orders` (list of dict): Each dict: `order_id`(int), `customer_name`(str), `order_date`(str), `total_amount`(float), `status`(str), `shipping_address`(str)
  - `status_filter` (str): One of "All", "Pending", "Shipped", "Delivered" (default "All")

- **Filtering**: Apply filter by `status` query parameter

---

### 8. Order Details Page (Optional but beneficial for `/order_history` view button)
- **Route Path**: `/order/<int:order_id>`
- **Function Name**: `order_details`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET
- **Template Rendered**: `order_details.html` (not explicitly requested in user task but inferred to view order details)
- **Context Variables**:
  - `order` (dict): Same fields as `orders` above
  - `order_items` (list of dict): Each dict: `order_item_id`(int), `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `quantity`(int), `price`(float), `subtotal`(float)

---

### 9. Reviews Page
- **Route Path**: `/reviews`
- **Function Name**: `reviews`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET
- **Template Rendered**: `reviews.html`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `reviews` (list of dict): Each dict: `review_id`(int), `book_title`(str), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str)
  - `rating_filter` (str): Rating filter from query param, e.g. "All", "5", "4", ...

- **Filtering**: Use `rating` query param to filter reviews

---

### 10. Write Review Page
- **Route Path**: `/write_review`
- **Function Name**: `write_review`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET, POST
- **Template Rendered**: `write_review.html`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `purchasable_books` (list of dict): Purchased books available for review with fields: `book_id`(int), `title`(str)

- **POST Handling**:
  - Form fields: `book_id` (int), `rating` (int 1-5), `review_text` (str), `customer_name` (Str, can be static or asked elsewise, no auth is specified, assumed user name submission with review or fixed name)
  - Append to `reviews.txt` with new review_id
  - Redirect to `/reviews`

---

### 11. Bestsellers Page
- **Route Path**: `/bestsellers`
- **Function Name**: `bestsellers`
- **HTTP Methods**: GET
- **Template Rendered**: `bestsellers.html`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `bestsellers` (list of dict): Each dict: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `sales_count`(int)
  - `time_period` (str): Filter by period from query param ("This Week", "This Month", "All Time")

- **Filtering**: Use query param for time period filter


---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### 1. Dashboard Page Template
- **File Path**: `templates/dashboard.html`
- **Page Title**: `Bookstore Dashboard`
- **Main H1**: `Bookstore Dashboard`
- **Element IDs**:
  - `dashboard-page` (Div): Container div for dashboard
  - `featured-books` (Div): Displays featured book recommendations
  - `browse-catalog-button` (Button): Navigates to `/catalog`
  - `view-cart-button` (Button): Navigates to `/cart`
  - `bestsellers-button` (Button): Navigates to `/bestsellers`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `featured_books` (list of dict)
  - `bestsellers` (list of dict)
- **Navigation**:
  - `browse-catalog-button` calls `url_for('catalog')`
  - `view-cart-button` calls `url_for('cart')`
  - `bestsellers-button` calls `url_for('bestsellers')`
- **Implementation notes**:
  - List featured books with title, author, and price inside `featured-books` div.
  - Display bestsellers (top ranked) with rank, title, author, sales count.

---

### 2. Book Catalog Page Template
- **File Path**: `templates/catalog.html`
- **Page Title**: `Book Catalog`
- **Main H1**: `Book Catalog`
- **Element IDs**:
  - `catalog-page` (Div): Container div
  - `search-input` (Input): Text input for search query
  - `category-filter` (Dropdown select): For category filtering
  - `books-grid` (Div): Holds book cards
  - Dynamic: `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): In each book card, to view details
- **Context Variables**:
  - `books` (list of dict)
  - `categories` (list of dict)
  - `selected_category` (str or None)
  - `search_query` (str or None)
- **Navigation**:
  - Book detail buttons use `url_for('book_details', book_id=book['book_id'])`
- **Filtering/Search**:
  - Search input and category dropdown submit on change or submit button to reload page with query params.

---

### 3. Book Details Page Template
- **File Path**: `templates/book_details.html`
- **Page Title**: `Book Details`
- **Main H1**: `book['title']` (dynamic)
- **Element IDs**:
  - `book-details-page` (Div): Container
  - `book-title` (H1): Displays book title dynamically
  - `book-author` (Div): Displays author
  - `book-price` (Div): Displays price
  - `add-to-cart-button` (Button): Adds book to cart via POST
  - `book-reviews` (Div): Lists customer reviews
- **Context Variables**:
  - `book` (dict)
  - `reviews` (list of dict)
- **POST Form**: 
  - Wrap the add to cart button inside a form with method POST.
  - Include hidden input for `book_id`.

---

### 4. Shopping Cart Page Template
- **File Path**: `templates/cart.html`
- **Page Title**: `Shopping Cart`
- **Main H1**: `Shopping Cart`
- **Element IDs**:
  - `cart-page` (Div): Container
  - `cart-items-table` (Table): Lists cart items with columns: Title, Quantity, Price, Subtotal
  - Dynamic inputs: `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input number) for quantity
  - Dynamic buttons: `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button) to remove item
  - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button): Navigates to `/checkout`
  - `total-amount` (Div): Displays total cart amount
- **Context Variables**:
  - `cart_items` (list of dict)
  - `total_amount` (float)
- **POST Form**:
  - Wrap the cart items table in a form with method POST.
  - Each quantity input named as `quantity_{cart_id}` to update quantities.
  - Each remove button named as `remove_{cart_id}`.

---

### 5. Checkout Page Template
- **File Path**: `templates/checkout.html`
- **Page Title**: `Checkout`
- **Main H1**: `Checkout`
- **Element IDs**:
  - `checkout-page` (Div): Container
  - `customer-name` (Input): For customer name
  - `shipping-address` (Textarea): For address
  - `payment-method` (Dropdown select): Options - Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer
  - `place-order-button` (Button): To submit form
- **Context Variables**:
  - `cart_items` (list of dict)
  - `total_amount` (float)
- **POST Form**:
  - All inputs and button inside a form method POST.

---

### 6. Order History Page Template
- **File Path**: `templates/order_history.html`
- **Page Title**: `Order History`
- **Main H1**: `Order History`
- **Element IDs**:
  - `orders-page` (Div): Container
  - `orders-table` (Table): Columns - Order ID, Date, Total Amount, Status
  - Dynamic buttons: `view-order-button-{order_id}`
  - `order-status-filter` (Dropdown): Filters by order status
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates to `/dashboard`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `orders` (list of dict)
  - `status_filter` (str)
- **Navigation**:
  - View order buttons link to `/order/<order_id>` (if implemented) or can be a placeholder.

---

### 7. Reviews Page Template
- **File Path**: `templates/reviews.html`
- **Page Title**: `Customer Reviews`
- **Main H1**: `Customer Reviews`
- **Element IDs**:
  - `reviews-page` (Div): Container
  - `reviews-list` (Div): Lists reviews with book title, rating, review text
  - `write-review-button` (Button): Navigates to `/write_review`
  - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown): Filters reviews by rating
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates to `/dashboard`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `reviews` (list of dict)
  - `rating_filter` (str)
- **Navigation**:
  - `write-review-button` calls `url_for('write_review')`

---

### 8. Write Review Page Template
- **File Path**: `templates/write_review.html`
- **Page Title**: `Write a Review`
- **Main H1**: `Write a Review`
- **Element IDs**:
  - `write-review-page` (Div): Container
  - `select-book` (Dropdown select): To select book to review
  - `rating-select` (Dropdown select): Ratings from 1 to 5
  - `review-text` (Textarea): For review text
  - `submit-review-button` (Button): Submit review
- **Context Variables**:
  - `purchasable_books` (list of dict)
- **POST Form**:
  - All inputs and submit button inside a form method POST.

---

### 9. Bestsellers Page Template
- **File Path**: `templates/bestsellers.html`
- **Page Title**: `Bestsellers`
- **Main H1**: `Bestsellers`
- **Element IDs**:
  - `bestsellers-page` (Div): Container
  - `bestsellers-list` (Div): Ranked list of bestsellers with rank, title, author, sales count
  - `time-period-filter` (Dropdown): Select period - This Week, This Month, All Time
  - Dynamic: `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): View book details
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigates to `/dashboard`
- **Context Variables**:
  - `bestsellers` (list of dict)
  - `time_period` (str)
- **Navigation**:
  - Buttons link to `url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)`

---

## Section 3: Data Schemas Specification

### 1. Books Data
- **File Location**: `data/books.txt`
- **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:
  ```
  book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description
  ```
- **Field Descriptions**:
  - `book_id` (int): Unique ID
  - `title` (str): Book title
  - `author` (str): Author name
  - `isbn` (str): ISBN number
  - `category` (str): Book category
  - `price` (float): Price in dollars
  - `stock` (int): Number of copies in stock
  - `description` (str): Short book description
- **Example Rows**:
  ```
  1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel
  2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind
  3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction
  ```

---

### 2. Categories Data
- **File Location**: `data/categories.txt`
- **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:
  ```
  category_id|category_name|description
  ```
- **Field Descriptions**:
  - `category_id` (int): Unique ID
  - `category_name` (str): Category name
  - `description` (str): Description of category
- **Example Rows**:
  ```
  1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels
  2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books
  3|Science|Scientific topics and research
  ```

---

### 3. Cart Data
- **File Location**: `data/cart.txt`
- **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:
  ```
  cart_id|book_id|quantity|added_date
  ```
- **Field Descriptions**:
  - `cart_id` (int): Unique cart item ID
  - `book_id` (int): Book reference
  - `quantity` (int): Quantity selected
  - `added_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD): Date added to cart
- **Example Rows**:
  ```
  1|1|2|2025-01-15
  2|3|1|2025-01-16
  ```

---

### 4. Orders Data
- **File Location**: `data/orders.txt`
- **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:
  ```
  order_id|customer_name|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address
  ```
- **Field Descriptions**:
  - `order_id` (int): Unique order ID
  - `customer_name` (str): Name of customer
  - `order_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD): Date of order
  - `total_amount` (float): Total order amount
  - `status` (str): Order status (Pending, Shipped, Delivered)
  - `shipping_address` (str): Shipping address
- **Example Rows**:
  ```
  1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001
  2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001
  ```

---

### 5. Order Items Data
- **File Location**: `data/order_items.txt`
- **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:
  ```
  order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price
  ```
- **Field Descriptions**:
  - `order_item_id` (int): Unique ID for order item
  - `order_id` (int): Related order ID
  - `book_id` (int): Book reference
  - `quantity` (int): Quantity ordered
  - `price` (float): Price at time of purchase
- **Example Rows**:
  ```
  1|1|1|2|12.99
  2|1|3|1|14.99
  3|2|2|1|16.99
  ```

---

### 6. Reviews Data
- **File Location**: `data/reviews.txt`
- **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:
  ```
  review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date
  ```
- **Field Descriptions**:
  - `review_id` (int): Unique review ID
  - `book_id` (int): Book reviewed
  - `customer_name` (str): Name of reviewer
  - `rating` (int): Rating 1 to 5
  - `review_text` (str): Text of review
  - `review_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD): Date of review
- **Example Rows**:
  ```
  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12
  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15
  ```

---

### 7. Bestsellers Data
- **File Location**: `data/bestsellers.txt`
- **Format**: Pipe (`|`) delimited, no header, fields in this exact order:
  ```
  book_id|sales_count|period
  ```
- **Field Descriptions**:
  - `book_id` (int): Book reference
  - `sales_count` (int): Number of sales
  - `period` (str): Time period (e.g., "This Week", "This Month", "All Time")
- **Example Rows**:
  ```
  2|150|This Month
  1|120|This Month
  3|95|This Month
  ```

---

# End of Design Specification

    <div id="bestsellers-page">
        <h1>Bestsellers</h1>

        <form method="get" action="{{ url_for('bestsellers') }}">
            <label for="time-period-filter">Select Time Period:</label>
            <select id="time-period-filter" name="time_period" onchange="this.form.submit()">
                <option value="This Week" {% if time_period == 'This Week' %}selected{% endif %}>This Week</option>
                <option value="This Month" {% if time_period == 'This Month' %}selected{% endif %}>This Month</option>
                <option value="All Time" {% if time_period == 'All Time' %}selected{% endif %}>All Time</option>
            </select>
        </form>

        <div id="bestsellers-list">
            <ol>
                {% for book in bestsellers %}
                    <li>
                        <strong>{{ loop.index }}. {{ book.title }}</strong> by {{ book.author }} - Sales: {{ book.sales_count }}
                        <button id="view-book-button-{{ book.book_id }}" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('book_details', book_id=book.book_id) }}'">View</button>
                    </li>
                {% else %}
                    <p>No bestseller data available.</p>
                {% endfor %}
            </ol>
        </div>

        <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
    </div>
</body>
</html>

item['added_date']\n        ])\n    write_pipe_file(CART_FILE, records)\n\n\ndef load_orders():\n    orders = []\n    raw = read_pipe_file(ORDERS_FILE, 6)\n    for parts in raw:\n        try:\n            order = {\n                'order_id': parse_int(parts[0]),\n                'customer_name': parts[1],\n                'order_date': parts[2],\n                'total_amount': parse_float(parts[3]),\n                'status': parts[4],\n                'shipping_address': parts[5]\n            }\n            orders.append(order)\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    return orders\n\n\ndef write_orders(orders):\n    records = []\n    for order in orders:\n        records.append([\n            order['order_id'],\n            order['customer_name'],\n            order['order_date'],\n            order['total_amount'],\n            order['status'],\n            order['shipping_address']\n        ])\n    write_pipe_file(ORDERS_FILE, records)\n\n\ndef load_order_items():\n    order_items = []\n    raw = read_pipe_file(ORDER_ITEMS_FILE, 5)\n    for parts in raw:\n        try:\n            oi = {\n                'order_item_id': parse_int(parts[0]),\n                'order_id': parse_int(parts[1]),\n                'book_id': parse_int(parts[2]),\n                'quantity': parse_int(parts[3]),\n                'price': parse_float(parts[4])\n            }\n            order_items.append(oi)\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    return order_items\n\n\ndef write_order_items(order_items):\n    records = []\n    for oi in order_items:\n        records.append([\n            oi['order_item_id'],\n            oi['order_id'],\n            oi['book_id'],\n            oi['quantity'],\n            oi['price']\n        ])\n    write_pipe_file(ORDER_ITEMS_FILE, records)\n\n\ndef load_reviews():\n    reviews = []\n    raw = read_pipe_file(REVIEWS_FILE, 6)\n    for parts in raw:\n        try:\n            review = {\n                'review_id': parse_int(parts[0]),\n                'book_id': parse_int(parts[1]),\n                'customer_name': parts[2],\n                'rating': parse_int(parts[3]),\n                'review_text': parts[4],\n                'review_date': parts[5]\n            }\n            reviews.append(review)\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    return reviews\n\n\ndef write_reviews(reviews):\n    records = []\n    for rev in reviews:\n        records.append([\n            rev['review_id'],\n            rev['book_id'],\n            rev['customer_name'],\n            rev['rating'],\n            rev['review_text'],\n            rev['review_date']\n        ])\n    write_pipe_file(REVIEWS_FILE, records)\n\n\ndef load_bestsellers():\n    bestsellers = []\n    raw = read_pipe_file(BESTSELLERS_FILE, 3)\n    for parts in raw:\n        try:\n            bs = {\n                'book_id': parse_int(parts[0]),\n                'sales_count': parse_int(parts[1]),\n                'period': parts[2]\n            }\n            bestsellers.append(bs)\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    return bestsellers\n\n\n# Route implementations\n\n# 1. Root route - redirect to dashboard\n@app.route('/')\ndef root_redirect():\n    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'), code=302)\n\n\n# 2. Dashboard\n@app.route('/dashboard')\ndef dashboard():\n    books = load_books()\n    bestsellers_raw = load_bestsellers()\n\n    # Featured books: top 5 books with stock > 0 (arbitrary choice)\n    featured_books = []\n    count = 0\n    for book in books:\n        if book['stock'] > 0:\n            featured_books.append({\n                'book_id': book['book_id'],\n                'title': book['title'],\n                'author': book['author'],\n                'price': book['price']\n            })\n            count += 1\n            if count >= 5:\n                break\n\n    # Get all time bestsellers for dashboard display (maybe top 5)\n    all_time_bs = [bs for bs in bestsellers_raw if bs['period'] == 'All Time']\n    # Sort descending by sales_count\n    all_time_bs_sorted = sorted(all_time_bs, key=lambda x: x['sales_count'], reverse=True)[:5]\n\n    # Prepare bestsellers info with title and author\n    bestsellers = []\n    # Create mapping from book_id to book\n    book_map = {b['book_id']: b for b in books}\n    for bs in all_time_bs_sorted:\n        b = book_map.get(bs['book_id'])\n        if b:\n            bestsellers.append({\n                'book_id': b['book_id'],\n                'title': b['title'],\n                'author': b['author'],\n                'sales_count': bs['sales_count']\n            })\n\n    return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_books=featured_books, bestsellers=bestsellers)\n\n\n# 3. Catalog\n@app.route('/catalog')\ndef catalog():\n    books = load_books()\n    categories = load_categories()\n\n    # Get query params\n    search_query = request.args.get('search', '').strip() or None\n    selected_category = request.args.get('category', '').strip() or None\n\n    filtered_books = books\n\n    if selected_category:\n        filtered_books = [b for b in filtered_books if b['category'].lower() == selected_category.lower()]\n\n    if search_query:\n        sq_lower = search_query.lower()\n        filtered_books = [b for b in filtered_books if (sq_lower in b['title'].lower()) or (sq_lower in b['author'].lower()) or (sq_lower in b['isbn'].lower())]\n\n    # Prepare minimal book info\n    books_info = []\n    for b in filtered_books:\n        books_info.append({\n            'book_id': b['book_id'],\n            'title': b['title'],\n            'author': b['author'],\n            'price': b['price']\n        })\n\n    # Provide category_names list\n    categories_info = []\n    for c in categories:\n        categories_info.append({\n            'category_id': c['category_id'],\n            'category_name': c['category_name']\n        })\n\n    return render_template('catalog.html', books=books_info, categories=categories_info, selected_category=selected_category, search_query=search_query)\n\n\n# 4. Book Details page\n@app.route('/book/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef book_details(book_id):\n    books = load_books()\n    book = None\n    for b in books:\n        if b['book_id'] == book_id:\n            book = b\n            break\n\n    if not book:\n        # Book not found - could abort 404\n        return 'Book not found', 404\n\n    reviews_all = load_reviews()\n    reviews_for_book = []\n    for r in reviews_all:\n        if r['book_id'] == book_id:\n            reviews_for_book.append({\n                'review_id': r['review_id'],\n                'customer_name': r['customer_name'],\n                'rating': r['rating'],\n                'review_text': r['review_text'],\n                'review_date': r['review_date']\n            })\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        # Processing add to cart\n        # The spec says triggered by 'add-to-cart-button' (button)\n        # We expect the form to submit with 'book_id' in form data\n\n        # Validate book_id matches url book_id\n        form_book_id = request.form.get('book_id')\n        if form_book_id and int(form_book_id) == book_id:\n            cart_items = load_cart()\n            # Check if item exists\n            found = False\n            for item in cart_items:\n                if item['book_id'] == book_id:\n                    # update quantity +1\n                    item['quantity'] += 1\n                    found = True\n                    break\n            if not found:\n                # Generate new cart_id; one more than max or 1 if empty\n                next_cart_id = 1\n                if cart_items:\n                    next_cart_id = max(i['cart_id'] for i in cart_items) + 1\n                cart_items.append({\n                    'cart_id': next_cart_id,\n                    'book_id': book_id,\n                    'quantity': 1,\n                    'added_date': get_today_date_str()\n                })\n            write_cart(cart_items)\n            # Redirect to same page to avoid form resubmission\n            return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))\n\n    return render_template('book_details.html', book=book, reviews=reviews_for_book)\n\n\n# 5. Shopping Cart page\n@app.route('/cart', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef cart():\n    books = load_books()\n    cart_items_raw = load_cart()\n    book_map = {b['book_id']: b for b in books}\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        # POST handling - update quantities or remove items\n        cart_items = load_cart()\n        # Process removal first\n        to_remove = set()\n\n        for key in request.form.keys():\n            if key.startswith('remove_'):\n                try:\n                    remove_id = int(key[len('remove_'):])\n                    to_remove.add(remove_id)\n                except Exception:\n                    continue\n\n        cart_items = [item for item in cart_items if item['cart_id'] not in to_remove]\n\n        # Process quantity updates\n        for key in request.form.keys():\n            if key.startswith('quantity_'):\n                try:\n                    cart_id = int(key[len('quantity_'):])\n                    quantity_val = int(request.form.get(key, '1'))\n                    if quantity_val < 1:\n                        quantity_val = 1\n                    # Update quantity if cart_id found\n                    for item in cart_items:\n                        if item['cart_id'] == cart_id:\n                            item['quantity'] = quantity_val\n                            break\n                except Exception:\n                    continue\n\n        write_cart(cart_items)\n        return redirect(url_for('cart'))\n\n    # Prepare context for GET\n    cart_items = []\n    total_amount = 0.0\n    for item in cart_items_raw:\n        b = book_map.get(item['book_id'])\n        if b:\n            quantity = item['quantity']\n            price = b['price']\n            subtotal = round(quantity * price, 2)\n            total_amount += subtotal\n            cart_items.append({\n                'cart_id': item['cart_id'],\n                'book_id': b['book_id'],\n                'title': b['title'],\n                'quantity': quantity,\n                'price': price,\n                'subtotal': subtotal\n            })\n\n    total_amount = round(total_amount, 2)\n\n    return render_template('cart.html', cart_items=cart_items, total_amount=total_amount)\n\n\n# 6. Checkout page\n@app.route('/checkout', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef checkout():\n    books = load_books()\n    cart_items_raw = load_cart()\n    book_map = {b['book_id']: b for b in books}\n\n    # Build cart_items for template\n    cart_items = []\n    total_amount = 0.0\n    for item in cart_items_raw:\n        b = book_map.get(item['book_id'])\n        if b:\n            quantity = item['quantity']\n            price = b['price']\n            subtotal = round(quantity * price, 2)\n            total_amount += subtotal\n            cart_items.append({\n                'cart_id': item['cart_id'],\n                'book_id': b['book_id'],\n                'title': b['title'],\n                'quantity': quantity,\n                'price': price,\n                'subtotal': subtotal\n            })\n\n    total_amount = round(total_amount, 2)\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        customer_name = request.form.get('customer_name', '').strip()\n        shipping_address = request.form.get('shipping_address', '').strip()\n        payment_method = request.form.get('payment_method', '').strip()\n\n        # Validate inputs\n        if not customer_name or not shipping_address or payment_method not in ['Credit Card', 'PayPal', 'Bank Transfer']:\n            # Bad request or re-render with error - for simplicity redirect to checkout\n            return redirect(url_for('checkout'))\n\n        if not cart_items:\n            # No items in cart - do nothing or redirect\n            return redirect(url_for('cart'))\n\n        # Load existing orders to find next order_id\n        orders = load_orders()\n        next_order_id = 1\n        if orders:\n            next_order_id = max(o['order_id'] for o in orders) + 1\n\n        order_date = get_today_date_str()\n\n        # Create the new order\n        new_order = {\n            'order_id': next_order_id,\n            'customer_name': customer_name,\n            'order_date': order_date,\n            'total_amount': total_amount,\n            'status': 'Pending',\n            'shipping_address': shipping_address\n        }\n        orders.append(new_order)\n\n        # Write orders\n        write_orders(orders)\n\n        # Add order items\n        order_items = load_order_items()\n        next_order_item_id = 1\n        if order_items:\n            next_order_item_id = max(oi['order_item_id'] for oi in order_items) + 1\n\n        for item in cart_items:\n            order_items.append({\n                'order_item_id': next_order_item_id,\n                'order_id': next_order_id,\n                'book_id': item['book_id'],\n                'quantity': item['quantity'],\n                'price': item['price']\n            })\n            next_order_item_id += 1\n\n        # Save order items\n        write_order_items(order_items)\n\n        # Clear cart\n        write_cart([])\n\n        # Redirect to order history\n        return redirect(url_for('order_history'))\n\n    return render_template('checkout.html', cart_items=cart_items, total_amount=total_amount)\n\n\n# 7. Order History Page\n@app.route('/order_history')\ndef order_history():\n    orders = load_orders()\n    status_filter = request.args.get('status', 'All')\n\n    if status_filter != 'All':\n        filtered_orders = [o for o in orders if o['status'].lower() == status_filter.lower()]\n    else:\n        filtered_orders = orders\n\n    return render_template('order_history.html', orders=filtered_orders, status_filter=status_filter)\n\n\n# 8. Order Details Page (Optional)\n@app.route('/order/<int:order_id>')\ndef order_details(order_id):\n    orders = load_orders()\n    order = None\n    for o in orders:\n        if o['order_id'] == order_id:\n            order = o\n            break\n    if not order:\n        return 'Order not found', 404\n\n    order_items_all = load_order_items()\n    books = load_books()\n    book_map = {b['book_id']: b for b in books}\n\n    order_items = []\n    for oi in order_items_all:\n        if oi['order_id'] == order_id:\n            b = book_map.get(oi['book_id'])\n            if b:\n                quantity = oi['quantity']\n                price = oi['price']\n                subtotal = round(quantity * price, 2)\n                order_items.append({\n                    'order_item_id': oi['order_item_id'],\n                    'book_id': oi['book_id'],\n                    'title': b['title'],\n                    'quantity': quantity,\n                    'price': price,\n                    'subtotal': subtotal\n                })\n\n    return render_template('order_details.html', order=order, order_items=order_items)\n\n\n# 9. Reviews Page\n@app.route('/reviews')\ndef reviews():\n    reviews_all = load_reviews()\n    books = load_books()\n    book_map = {b['book_id']: b for b in books}\n\n    rating_filter = request.args.get('rating', 'All')\n\n    filtered_reviews = []\n    for r in reviews_all:\n        if rating_filter == 'All' or str(r['rating']) == rating_filter:\n            book = book_map.get(r['book_id'])\n            book_title = book['title'] if book else 'Unknown'\n            filtered_reviews.append({\n                'review_id': r['review_id'],\n                'book_title': book_title,\n                'rating': r['rating'],\n                'review_text': r['review_text']\n            })\n\n    return render_template('reviews.html', reviews=filtered_reviews, rating_filter=rating_filter)\n\n\n# 10. Write Review Page\n@app.route('/write_review', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef write_review():\n    orders = load_orders()\n    order_items = load_order_items()\n    books = load_books()\n\n    # We want purchasable_books - unique books from past orders\n    purchased_book_ids = set(oi['book_id'] for oi in order_items)\n    purchased_books = [b for b in books if b['book_id'] in purchased_book_ids]\n\n    # Remove duplicates if any\n    unique_books = {}\n    for b in purchased_books:\n        unique_books[b['book_id']] = b\n    purchasable_books = list(unique_books.values())\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        book_id_str = request.form.get('book_id')\n        rating_str = request.form.get('rating')\n        review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()\n        customer_name = request.form.get('customer_name', '').strip()\n\n        # Validate inputs\n        try:\n            book_id = int(book_id_str)\n            rating = int(rating_str)\n            if rating < 1 or rating > 5:\n                raise ValueError('Rating out of range')\n        except Exception:\n            return redirect(url_for('write_review'))\n\n        if not customer_name or not review_text:\n            return redirect(url_for('write_review'))\n\n        # Validate book_id is in purchasable_books\n        if book_id not in unique_books:\n            return redirect(url_for('write_review'))\n\n        # Generate new review_id\n        reviews_all = load_reviews()\n        next_review_id = 1\n        if reviews_all:\n            next_review_id = max(r['review_id'] for r in reviews_all) + 1\n\n        review_date = get_today_date_str()\n\n        new_review = {\n            'review_id': next_review_id,\n            'book_id': book_id,\n            'customer_name': customer_name,\n            'rating': rating,\n            'review_text': review_text,\n            'review_date': review_date\n        }\n\n        reviews_all.append(new_review)\n        write_reviews(reviews_all)\n\n        return redirect(url_for('reviews'))\n\n    return render_template('write_review.html', purchasable_books=purchasable_books)\n\n\n# 11. Bestsellers Page\n@app.route('/bestsellers')\ndef bestsellers():\n    time_period = request.args.get('time_period', 'All Time')\n    bestsellers_all = load_bestsellers()\n    books = load_books()\n    book_map = {b['book_id']: b for b in books}\n\n    filtered_bs = [bs for bs in bestsellers_all if bs['period'] == time_period]\n\n    # Sort descending by sales_count\n    filtered_bs_sorted = sorted(filtered_bs, key=lambda x: x['sales_count'], reverse=True)\n\n    bestsellers = []\n    for bs in filtered_bs_sorted:\n        b = book_map.get(bs['book_id'])\n        if b:\n            bestsellers.append({\n                'book_id': b['book_id'],\n                'title': b['title'],\n                'author': b['author'],\n                'sales_count': bs['sales_count']\n            })\n\n    return render_template('bestsellers.html', bestsellers=bestsellers, time_period=time_period)\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app.run(debug=True)\n"})
